        <li> For Stream-Stream joins, all three types (inner, outer, left) handle out-of-order records correctly.</li>\\n336:         <li> For Stream-Table joins, if not using versioned stores, then         <li> For Stream-Stream joins, all three types (inner, outer, left) handle out-of-order records correctly.</li>\n336:         <li> For Stream-Table joins, if not using versioned stores, then The codebase does not currently show explicit v1/v2 versioning, but rather a single modern API version.\\n\\n### Key Resource Handlers\\n\\n**Primary Connector Resource Handler:**\\n- **ConnectorsResource** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/resources/ConnectorsResource.java)\\n  - Main REST endpoint for connector management\\n  - Path: `/connectors`\\n  - Handles operations: create, read, update, delete, restart, pause, resume connectors\\n  - Methods for task management: getTaskConfigs, getTaskStatus, restartTask\\n  - Methods for connector status: getConnectorStatus, listConnectors\\n\\n**Supporting Resource Handlers:**\\n- **RootResource** - Root endpoint (`/`) providing server info and health checks\\n- **InternalConnectResource** - Inter-worker communication for internal requests\\n- **InternalClusterResource** - Parent class for internal cluster operations (putTaskConfigs, fenceZombies)\\n- **ConnectorPluginsResource** - Plugin discovery and validation endpoint\\n- **LoggingResource** - Dynamic logging management endpoint\\n\\n### Task Status and Error Response Schemas\\n\\n**Task Status Schema (ConnectorStateInfo.TaskState):**\\n- Location: connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/entities/ConnectorStateInfo.java\\n- Fields:\\n  - `id` (int): Task ID\\n  - `state` (String): Task state (e.g., 'running', 'paused', 'failed', 'restarting')\\n  - `worker_id` (String): ID of the worker running the task\\n  - `trace` (String): Error trace (optional, included only when non-empty)\\n  - `version` (String): Plugin version information (filtered to exclude when not set)\\n- Parent class: AbstractState - defines common state information for both connectors and tasks\\n\\n**Connector Status Schema (ConnectorStateInfo.ConnectorState):**\\n- Extends AbstractState with same fields as TaskState\\n- Fields:\\n  - `state` (String): Connector state\\n  - `worker_id` (String): Worker ID\\n  - `msg` (String): Error message (mapped from trace)\\n  - `version` (String): Plugin version\\n\\n**Error Response Schema (ErrorMessage):**\\n- Location: connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/entities/ErrorMessage.java\\n- Fields:\\n  - `error_code` (int): HTTP status code or error code\\n  - `message` (String): Error description\\n- Generated automatically by ConnectExceptionMapper for uncaught exceptions\\n\\n### Error Handling Architecture\\n\\n**ConnectRestException** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/errors/ConnectRestException.java)\\n- Extends ConnectException\\n- Contains `statusCode` (int): HTTP status code\\n- Contains `errorCode` (int): Semantic error code\\n- Mapped to ErrorMessage by ConnectExceptionMapper\\n\\n**ConnectExceptionMapper** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/errors/ConnectExceptionMapper.java)\\n- Implements jakarta.ws.rs.ext.ExceptionMapper<Exception>\\n- Maps exceptions to REST responses with ErrorMessage body\\n- Handles: ConnectRestException, NotFoundException, AlreadyExistsException, WebApplicationException\\n\\n### Version Routing and Request Handling\\n\\n**RestServer Infrastructure:**\\n- **RestServer** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/RestServer.java) - Abstract base class managing Jetty server setup and resource registration\\n- **ConnectRestServer** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/ConnectRestServer.java) - Concrete implementation registering ConnectorsResource, RootResource, InternalConnectResource, ConnectorPluginsResource, and LoggingResource\\n\\n**Request Processing:**\\n- HerderRequestHandler manages request completion and forwarding between workers\\n- RestClient handles inter-worker HTTP communication\\n- RestServerConfig provides configuration for REST API behavior\\n\\n### Key Implementation Details\\n\\n**Task Status Endpoint:**\\n- GET `/connectors/{connector}/tasks/{task}/status` returns ConnectorStateInfo.TaskState\\n- Includes worker_id, state, trace (when error), and version information\\n\\n**Connector Status Endpoint:**\\n- GET `/connectors/{connector}/status` returns ConnectorStateInfo with connector state and task states array\\n- Provides comprehensive status of all tasks for a connector\\n\\n**Version Field:**\\n- Both TaskState and ConnectorState include a `version` field for plugin version tracking\\n- Uses custom JsonInclude filter (PluginInfo.NoVersionFilter) to exclude null/empty versions from response\\n\\n### API Design Patterns\\n\\n1. **JAX-RS/Jersey-based:** Uses Jakarta EE REST annotations (@Path, @GET, @POST, @PUT, @DELETE)\\n2. **JSON Serialization:** Jackson for automatic JSON serialization/deserialization\\n3. **OpenAPI Support:** Uses io.swagger.v3 annotations for OpenAPI documentation\\n4. **Dependency Injection:** Uses Jakarta Inject for component binding\\n5. **Request Forwarding:** Supports internal worker-to-worker request forwarding via HerderRequestHandler\\n\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":11,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1347,"cache_read_input_tokens":107468,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1347},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"66a1f9d7-94b7-4d71-bbb5-fa13f0ef85e9","uuid":"4a9c1de0-4a2a-45b0-93f5-a1f87dc773e0"}

I've completed a comprehensive analysis of the Kafka Connect REST API implementation in the Apache Kafka repository. Here's a summary of what I found:\n\n## Key Findings\n\n### REST API Resource Handlers\nThe Kafka Connect REST API is implemented through several resource classes:\n- **ConnectorsResource** - Main handler for connector management endpoints (`/connectors`)\n- **RootResource** - Server info and health check endpoints\n- **InternalConnectResource** - Inter-worker communication\n- **ConnectorPluginsResource** - Plugin discovery and validation\n- **LoggingResource** - Dynamic logging management\n\n### Task Status Schema (ConnectorStateInfo.TaskState)\nLocated in `connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/entities/ConnectorStateInfo.java`, the task status includes:\n- `id` (int) - Task ID\n- `state` (String) - Current state (running, paused, failed, restarting)\n- `worker_id` (String) - Worker identifier\n- `trace` (String) - Error message when applicable\n- `version` (String) - Plugin version information\n\n### Error Response Schema (ErrorMessage)\nLocated in `connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/entities/ErrorMessage.java`, with fields:\n- `error_code` (int) - HTTP status or error code\n- `message` (String) - Error description\n\n### Version Routing\nThe implementation uses a single unified REST API interface without explicit v1/v2 routes.
